## 1. `admission.Interface` Registration

These files define the core interfaces every plugin must satisfy and the registry that maps plugin names to factory functions.

### Core interfaces
**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/interfaces.go`**
The single most important file in the pipeline. Declares every interface a plugin can implement:
| Symbol | Role |
|---|---|
| `Interface` | Base: `Handles(Operation) bool` |
| `MutationInterface` | Adds `Admit(ctx, Attributes, ObjectInterfaces) error` |
| `ValidationInterface` | Adds `Validate(ctx, Attributes, ObjectInterfaces) error` |
| `InitializationValidator` | `ValidateInitialization() error` — called after all `PluginInitializer.Initialize` calls |
| `PluginInitializer` | `Initialize(plugin Interface)` — dependency-injection contract |
| `PluginInitializers` | Slice of `PluginInitializer`; its own `Initialize` fans out to each member |
| `Attributes` | Per-request context passed to every `Admit`/`Validate` call |
| `ObjectInterfaces` | Scheme-level helpers (creator, typer, convertor, defaulter) |

**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/handler.go`**
| Symbol | Role |
|---|---|
| `Handler` | Embeddable base struct every plugin embeds; holds the `Operations` bitmask and a `readyFunc` |
| `NewHandler(ops ...Operation)` | Constructor; sets which operations the plugin handles |
| `WaitForReady()` | Blocks until `readyFunc` returns true (used by informer-backed plugins) |
| `SetReadyFunc(f func() bool)` | Lets initializers inject the readiness 
... (truncated)

The ordering within each phase is determined by `AllOrderedPlugins` in `pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go`. Mutating webhooks use **sequential ordered iteration with reinvocation**; validating webhooks use **parallel fan-out with no reinvocation**."
